                                                  <div data-reactid="2">
                                                    Our home has recently been updated although still a WIP! Perfect for those interested in a quiet/private sweet retreat with a stunning private view of the Santa Rosa Mts. Enjoy hiking/walking, dip in the pool, sip a cocktail, shop or make a spa rez.
                                                  </div>
                                                  <div data-reactid="3">
                                                    Our private Mid Century home, in the heart of the Magnesia Falls Cove, is your new seasonal R&amp;R getaway. Simply decorated, it has all the comforts of home. Our backyard sits in the Santa Rosa Mts w incredible views from the new pool and spa! Coachella Valley is home to the Santa Rosa Mountains, where granite, desert flora, and sweeping views surround primo hiking.

We are working on this house every chance we get! Both the physical side of the home as well as the amenities side of things. We love to travel so we will do our best to implement what we love and appreciate.

Our space is considered a hidden gem - you can not beat our location and peace and quiet! Tucked against the  base of the Santa Rosa mountains, you have direct &amp; personal access to the Rancho Mirage "Bump-n-Grind" trail which has quickly becoming one of Coachella Valley's most popular trails for biking, hiking, walking at any time of day. You can also view the people walking the trails from our backyard so people watching from afar can be fun too.

The home itself has brand new polished concrete floors, modern furniture, lots of glass and traditional eyebrow windows, it is full of natural light and offers beautiful panoramic views from the house and backyard. The space is private, quiet and peaceful, the water is such a treat and you can enjoy a walk or hike anytime. At sunrise, you can catch a pretty incredible, unobstructed view from the patio, pool or hot tub.

We haven't had a chance to remodel the entire thing so we'd like to share with others who are looking for a simple, sweet retreat. Set a t-time for golf, watch tennis at Indian Wells Tennis Gardens, enjoy a sports game on our 65 in TV. Visit Joshua Tree National Park, dip in the pool, enjoy a few homemade cocktails or make a spa reservation nearby. This is absolutely the best bang for your buck!
                                                  </div>
                                                  <div data-reactid="4">
                                                    You will be in the community of Magnesia Falls Cove. Hwy 111 between Bob Hope &amp; Fred Warning. Nestled between Palm Springs/Catherdral City and Indian Wells/La Quinta/Coachella, you're truly in the very best area! Brand new commercial construction is finishing up at the end of our street - great location!!

You can walk to The River for shopping, dinner, cocktails, even a movie! The Rancho Las Palmas Resort is just across the street from The River with an 18-hole golf course, fine dining and a full service spa. Step out through the backyard straight onto Coachella Valley's prized &amp; world renowned Bump n' Grind hiking trail for a morning walk/bike ride or evening scenic hike. The backyard is updated and an absolute oasis with pool and hot tub!

We share lovely conversation and walks. It was generous of her to share her lovely yard and the fruits from her garden. Tomato, tangerine, grapefruit and lemons. All organic. I will definitely visit her again when in Rancho Mirage.  Thanks Ethal.  Flora

Location is quiet central for what we needed: hiking, golf, groceries, restaurants so that was nice. Ethel is an easy person to talk to and was quite accommodating.     The rooms were fine / basic but did the trick for us. Given it's November the pool was quite cold (we still jumped in quickly) and the fruit on the trees weren't ripe yet but nothing we can do about that except change our trip dates in Feb/March. Don't expect the Ritz but if you're looking for a nice, quiet place to relax for a few days this will suffice.

                                                  <div data-reactid="2">
                                                    Gorgeous home in spectacular neighborhood, where every house is a work of art. Centrally located, short drive to The  BNP Paribas Open, Coachella, Stagecoach, Modernism Week, Palm Springs International Film Festival -everything going on here year-round. Palm Springs airport's 8 miles away, a short 20 minute drive &amp; you're here! Private setting with sauna, pool facing mountains. Extremely desirable spot for seasonal use, and great pricing for this home at $3900 per month during high  season.
                                                  </div>
                                                  <div data-reactid="3">
                                                    This house is truly a desert oasis - the most likely sound you will hear is the sound of birds chirping. It's a very clean, quiet neighborhood and pride of ownership is evident throughout. Super cozy, yet the layout makes the home very spacious.

Super elegant yet cozy Mid - Century Modern home in the desirable Magnesia Falls Cove area of Rancho Mirage. If you like stunning mountain views, eye - catching art, high end furnishings and luxury linens then this is the place for you!    The home is a very spacious 1500 square feet with 2 large bedrooms and two full bathrooms, as well as a smaller third bedroom which serves as a cozy room for a single, furnished with  a super comfortable Euro-plush Stearns and Foster twin mattress and ample storage. This room also makes a great office. The pool is designed with iridescent tiles imported from Japan in a striking original pattern that fits right in with the days of Elvis Presley and the Rat Pack. Large, ultra glamorous private back area with freshly tiled patio make this a perfect place to entertain friends or just relax and enjoy the beautiful mountain views and lush palm trees.
There are numerous great restaurants and shops within walking distance in The River complex, as well as a multitude of golf courses and tennis courts to enjoy. Hiking and cycling are popular activities here as well. I have been hosting on Airbnb for almost 5 years, and have many great reviews that can be seen through my San Francisco, New York and Rancho MIrage listings. The home is ideal for couples traveling together, as both bedrooms are on opposite sides of the house and the guest bedroom has it's own entrance, affording complete privacy. Please note, the property is for adults only and not suitable for small children. Please contact me to discuss your situation if traveling with grown children.  I am super excited about it, and I am sure when you see it, you will be too! Come check it out!

I have a few simple rules that I hope guests follow. No smoking please and no pets. Please remove shoes in the house. No wet towels on furniture, wood chairs, beds, etc. There are drying racks in each closet for your use or outdoor drying

The mountain views are amazing, and the air is so clear here you can always see the stars at night!

There is a bus about 5  minutes walking distance that will take you up and down Highway 111 so getting around by public transit is an option. You can also rent bicycles in the area and this is a very popular place with cyclists.
